<div id="review_220221967" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220221967" />
    <a title="shady boots" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4972138-shady-boots"><img alt="shady boots" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592459241p2/4972138.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220221967?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="shady boots" class="user" itemprop="url" name="shady boots" href="/user/show/4972138-shady-boots">shady boots</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=meh-it-was-okay">meh-it-was-okay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=boooooring">boooooring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=dont-understand-why-its-hyped">dont-understand-why-its-hyped</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220221967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15634577273444302780">This review is also available on <a href='http://wildheartbookblogs.blogspot.com/2012/04/review-night-school-by-cj-daugherty.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>my blog.</a><br/><br/>__________________________________<br/><br/>I can't think of a rating for this. Either 3, 3.5, 3.75, I just don't know.<br/><br/>So I decided to get this book because the reviews I've seen gave it the impression that this is a book of pure epicness. I was intrigued and curious, so I was excited when I managed to get my hands on it.<br/><br/>Unfortunately, it kind of let me down.<br/><br/>So this book is about Allie Sheridan who became a rebellious girl after her older brother Christopher ran aw</span>
  <span id="freeText15634577273444302780" style="display:none">This review is also available on <a href="http://wildheartbookblogs.blogspot.com/2012/04/review-night-school-by-cj-daugherty.html" rel="nofollow noopener">my blog.</a><br><br>__________________________________<br><br>I can't think of a rating for this. Either 3, 3.5, 3.75, I just don't know.<br><br>So I decided to get this book because the reviews I've seen gave it the impression that this is a book of pure epicness. I was intrigued and curious, so I was excited when I managed to get my hands on it.<br><br>Unfortunately, it kind of let me down.<br><br>So this book is about Allie Sheridan who became a rebellious girl after her older brother Christopher ran away from home. Her parents send her to Cimmeria Academy, a pretty strict private school. And then lies and secrets galore.<br><br>This book is shelved as paranormal, and to be honest, I have no idea why. Because I didn't find a single paranormal aspect to it. Sure, there's tons of mystery in it, but mystery and paranormal are <i>very</i> different genres. Was there maybe something I missed or what? Could someone please explain to me why this is categorized as paranormal?<br><br>So anyway, at first this book was pretty fun to read. I liked Allie and other characters as well. After a few pages, though, it started to drag. And drag. And drag.<br><br>And drag some more.<br><br>Yes, I did get bored with it. There weren't many things in this book that made it stick out from other YA books out there. For instance, there's the two hot guys pining for the same girl. And of course the girl picks the smoldering bad boy with the soft side, cause they <i>always</i> do. The good guy turns out to be a jerk.<br><br>There were some scenes that kept me interested, but I was very disappointed at the end, because nothing even happened. I kept expecting for something <i>huge</i> to happen, like maybe finally the big reveal of why this book is categorized as paranormal. But no. Nothing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360780ra/711682.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I did want to love this book, but it was hard to. I just didn't see anything special about it. :/ Sure, I guess it's a good book, but I wasn't expecting a good book. I was expecting a <i>fantastic</i> book, and that's why I'm pretty disappointed.<br><br>Don't take my word for it, though.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15634577273444302780" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_249287420" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/249287420" />
    <a title="Jessie  (Ageless Pages Reviews)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews"><img alt="Jessie  (Ageless Pages Reviews)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603380977p2/4863162.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/249287420?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessie  (Ageless Pages Reviews)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessie  (Ageless Pages Reviews)" href="/user/show/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews">Jessie  (Ageless Pages Reviews)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062193858" href="/book/show/16103765-night-school">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=ya-fiction">ya-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=edelweiss-arc">edelweiss-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=reviews-2013">reviews-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=bring-on-the-cliche-parade">bring-on-the-cliche-parade</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=blah-blah-blaaahhhh">blah-blah-blaaahhhh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=coverlove">coverlove</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=looks-can-be-deceiving">looks-can-be-deceiving</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4863162-jessie-ageless-pages-reviews?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer249287420" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5487936820616479194"><b>Read <a href='http://agelesspagesreviews.blogspot.com/2013/05/review-night-school-by-cj-daugherty.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>This Review</a> & More Like It <a href='http://agelesspagesreviews.blogspot.com/"' rel='nofollow noopener'>On My Blog</a>!</b><br/><br/>C.J. Daugherty has several things going for her in her debut novel and the first in her Night School series: a chilling, thoroughly Gothic vibe, an interesting and just-convoluted-enough conspiracy theory, and a somewhat rounded main character. Unfortunately for both <i>Night School</i> and its readers, Daugherty loses sight of what she should write about and focuses on mean girls, petty high school drama, "mysterious" boys, and an obnoxious love trianle with </span>
  <span id="freeText5487936820616479194" style="display:none"><b>Read <a href="http://agelesspagesreviews.blogspot.com/2013/05/review-night-school-by-cj-daugherty.html" rel="nofollow noopener">This Review</a> &amp; More Like It <a href="http://agelesspagesreviews.blogspot.com/&quot;" rel="nofollow noopener">On My Blog</a>!</b><br /><br />C.J. Daugherty has several things going for her in her debut novel and the first in her Night School series: a chilling, thoroughly Gothic vibe, an interesting and just-convoluted-enough conspiracy theory, and a somewhat rounded main character. Unfortunately for both <i>Night School</i> and its readers, Daugherty loses sight of what she should write about and focuses on mean girls, petty high school drama, "mysterious" boys, and an obnoxious love trianle with Allie at the center. There are kernels of good ideas at play in the novel, but but so much of what's worth time and attention gets lost in the morass of overwritten drama that takes center stage.<br /><br />Allie is a...decent protagonist. She's serviceable, I guess. That's the best I can do with what Daugherty gave me. She had her moments where I wanted to shake her (any time she is swooning over either a creepy or a borderline abusive love interest) but she also had moments where she took a stand (at the dance? With Sylvain? Hell yeah. Unfortunately as the even gets further behind her, Allie gets more forgiving...) and I found myself caring about her. Still, there are multiple issues with Allie's characterization. <i>Of course</i> two totally hot, mysterious and unattainable guys are in love with Allie. Of course. How utterly unexpected. It's just so trite and overdone, and Allie's interactions with both highlight how much more interested <i>Night School</i> is in silly romance and teenage relationships than it is in crafting a taut thriller/conspiracy novel.<br /><br />It also doesn't help <i>Night School</i> that there are so many plotlines left open and questions unanswered by the final page. It's a frustrating experience for a reader to invest so much time in a four-hundred page novel that, due to those unsatisfying factors, ends up being nothing more than a lengthy introduction; one with little to no resolution. I had trouble with this until very close to the end. The endless mysteries and secrets that EVERYONE besides Allie is in on, the unexplained caste system between the Night School students and the regular students... it did nothing for me. My experience did get slightly better, towards the very end but the utter lack of any resolution is very, very frustrating.<br /><br />I have Concerns about Cimmeria Academy. (First: what kind of school would provide alcohol - their own brand! - to students at a school dance, hosted at the school? What?!) The author deliberately paints the school in broad strokes; all the better to make her audience curious about its endgame with the students. What is Night School? Why are only some students involved? How are they picked? What do they do? -All of which set up more with expectations than the actual reveal can deliver. When you find out the point, or the barest outline of the point of Night School that is shown in the first book, it's a let down, pure and simple. There's not enough there there; the knowledge imparted to Allie is minimal, and laughable. It comes across as a desperate ploy to ensure continued reading and frustrated me even more. <br /><br />The complete lack of a reason for the antagonists motivation also is ridiculous. Readers are just supposed to get that he wants Something and It Is Very Dangerous and he will do anything to get it. Why? What lead up to that and what he does in the book? If you haven't even cracked the cover, you know just as much as I do, four hundred pages later. No one - at least no one interesting and worth reading about, is evil for evil's sake. Give me a villain with reasons, intelligence and believable motivations and you've just upped the appeal of your book. For all that, the minor antagonist? From the events at the dance? That revelation did manage to surprise me, and even if I can't wholly buy into why they did what they did (again: no answers, no real motivations shown), I can appreciate how ably the author pulled it off.<br /><br />There are some obvious issues with <i>Night School</i>. For all that, I did enjoy aspects of it. The Gothic vibe works well for the story, Allie isn't a complete waste of space, and it's a pretty readable novel. It may be more work that its worth, but then again, I can't promise I won't be drawn into reading the sequel, <i>Legacy</i>, when it comes out. The contents of the first Night School novel can't quite live up to the premise (or that awesome cover) but it's not a complete mess. It just gets lost in the mundane and neglects the ideas and themes that could have made it truly original. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5487936820616479194" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer504904865" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1634001420467699058">Night School was recommended to me by my good friend Tina. She told me not read any spoilers, to go in knowing as little as possible and I am so glad I listened to her. Becaused it was so different from what I was expecting but I mean that in a good way. Now I don't want to say anything about what this book was actually about because it is nice to have a book that takes you by surprise. Let just say it was intriguing plot. I loved the mystery too it and how it leaves me with questions that I des</span>
  <span id="freeText1634001420467699058" style="display:none">Night School was recommended to me by my good friend Tina. She told me not read any spoilers, to go in knowing as little as possible and I am so glad I listened to her. Becaused it was so different from what I was expecting but I mean that in a good way. Now I don't want to say anything about what this book was actually about because it is nice to have a book that takes you by surprise. Let just say it was intriguing plot. I loved the mystery too it and how it leaves me with questions that I desperately want to know the answers too. <br /><br />What let this book down for me were the characters. Some of them seemed a bit sterotypical (you know the mean girl, the dark brooding guy, the guy every girl loves etc) and some of them made stupid decisions. I have such mixed feelings about them. I just haven't quite figured them out. Allie the main character was okay. I am hoping she becomes stronger and a little bit more mature in the next book. I like Carter but I think we need more of his story. But Sylvain he confused me so much. I am not sure if I like him or not. The same goes for Jo and Jules. <br /><br />Overall, even though the character could at times be annoying I couldn't stop turning the pages. I want more, I want answers to my questions, so I am off to read book two right away! </span>

    <a title="Novels On The Run" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4119908-novels-on-the-run"><img alt="Novels On The Run" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281183501p2/4119908.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/255401319?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Novels On The Run" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Novels On The Run" href="/user/show/4119908-novels-on-the-run">Novels On The Run</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer255401319" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10297509358661603994">MICHELLE'S REVIEW:<br/><br/>RATING : 4.5 MOODY CARTER STARS!!<br/><br/>“Never be afraid to be honest.”<br/><br/>New series alert!! *flashing red light*<br/><br/>This is the series to look out for. I received this book from Atom and I knew I was going to like it. I love a good Academy book. Cimmeria Academy ( I need me somebody to tell me how to pronounce it!) has mystery , murder and some mayhem and boys, boys, boys!!( so very important, hee..hee) and of course the bitchy girl...you have to have a bitchy girl, they can be so much fun </span>
  <span id="freeText10297509358661603994" style="display:none">MICHELLE'S REVIEW:<br /><br />RATING : 4.5 MOODY CARTER STARS!!<br /><br />“Never be afraid to be honest.”<br /><br />New series alert!! *flashing red light*<br /><br />This is the series to look out for. I received this book from Atom and I knew I was going to like it. I love a good Academy book. Cimmeria Academy ( I need me somebody to tell me how to pronounce it!) has mystery , murder and some mayhem and boys, boys, boys!!( so very important, hee..hee) and of course the bitchy girl...you have to have a bitchy girl, they can be so much fun to read. <br /><br />Night School is a little slow at first, but then the rip cord has been pulled and there is this constant urge to turn pages and find out what is going on with the characters and Cimmeria Academy.<br /><br />Now, the jury is still out on if this is a paranormal series and Ms. Daugherty has left me guessing for sure. You have to read this book to see what I mean. There are hints or suggestions but I am still mystified as to what we are playing with here. This is not a bad thing. Or am I reading too much into it. Don’t be fooled by the title, it may not mean what you think...or does it? I have my suspicions, but.......<br /><br />We have Sylvain, the French dude who is from an uber, uber, uber rich , old, powerful family, we are talking Billions here. Now, he doesn’t mind the ladies but, he has zoomed in on our main gal Allie, Alyson Sheridan. Why?<br /><br />All is not what it seems.....<br /><br />Enter Carter West, moody, ( Bingo! I always love a moody guy, because eventually when that moodiness drops...*sigh*...the goods are revealed), cranky, yet poetic, he also gets a fair bit of detention. Bad boy image, but is he? <br /><br />Gabe is the current squeeze of Jo ( she has a rather interesting character) , he and Carter aren’t buds but they have a common ground at the Academy.<br /><br />Isabelle is the Head Mistress of Cimmeria and there are a lot of secrets within the walls of the academy. There is no 21st Century within it’s walls. No laptops, Ipods. Pen, paper and a desk ( which comes in rather handy) are all you need and rules, lots of rules to keep the secrets, secret.<br /><br />Lots of great sub characters to get to know, Lucas, Jules, Ruth, Phil, Lisa, some skinny dipping peeps....ha!<br /><br />Allie is a bit of a rebel, she has her reasons and she is hurting on the inside. Christopher, her brother who she was very close to has disappeared. Allie spirals out of control... 3 arrests later and her parents just happen to choose Cimmeria to send her off to.<br /><br />Allie is a bit of a mystery to the other students at Cimmeria, trust is a big issue and she finds herself lifting the lid on things she should have left well alone. I love her flaws and the way she counts everything when feeling like she may be losing it or a panic attack is on the horizon. Allie’s character starts to grow, mature in this book, take charge of her life and not be so damaging. Trouble follows her in this book at every turn, but she is learning.<br /><br />Sylvain is a very secretive and alluring character at first......but..... then needs a ‘stinky dead fish’ slap from me, but then.....something changes. Is it possibly genuine regret?<br /><br />I just love Carter and Rachel. Carter is my Team T-shirt guy.<br /><br />I am rather desperate for book 2 as there is this mystery still left open. I think this party has only just got started and I want another all access pass. <br /><br />Trust is a bit of a dirty word in this book and the secrets.......just don’t be caught telling them!<br /><br />An awesome start to this series.... my mind boggles where it will be going as there is mystery, mystery, mystery....<br /><br />FAVE QUOTE:<br /><br />“Has anybody ever mentioned you’ve got an exaggeration problem?” he said.<br />“No,” Allie replied. “Anybody ever mention you’ve got a dickhead problem?”<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_207016494" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/207016494" />
    <a title="Brodie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2748076-brodie"><img alt="Brodie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1549082975p2/2748076.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/207016494?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brodie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brodie" href="/user/show/2748076-brodie">Brodie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2748076-brodie?shelf=2012">2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2748076-brodie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer207016494" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10699822805409365942">Allie's screwed up for the last time. Her parents are tired of her being expelled from school or arrested by the police. Ever since her brother went missing, she's fallen into a downward spiral. So when her parents ship her off to Cimmeria Academy, a boarding school where only legacy or the best of the best attend, Allie isn't expecting to life to get better. To her surprise, she quickly settles in and makes a few friends. But she soon learns that a darkness lurks in the heart of Cimmeria as sec</span>
  <span id="freeText10699822805409365942" style="display:none">Allie's screwed up for the last time. Her parents are tired of her being expelled from school or arrested by the police. Ever since her brother went missing, she's fallen into a downward spiral. So when her parents ship her off to Cimmeria Academy, a boarding school where only legacy or the best of the best attend, Allie isn't expecting to life to get better. To her surprise, she quickly settles in and makes a few friends. But she soon learns that a darkness lurks in the heart of Cimmeria as secrets, murder and twisting danger erupt. What exactly is the mysterious Night School and what do its members get up to in the dead of the night?<br /><br />Allie is the kind of heroine you will easily warm to. She's fun, stubborn and pretty level-headed... which given the arrests I mentioned above, you might find hard to believe, but once she settles in to Cimmeria, I really felt like she handled things well. Which is helpful, considering she's about to get tangled up in some heavy stuff. And oh, Carter! I loved him! While at first he was mysterious and standoffish, I so enjoyed seeing his sweet personality shine through more. He compelled me, despite being frustratingly vague with Allie at times. I was desperate to learn more about him and for any scene in which he interacted with her. There was clear sexual tension developing between those two and I loved their arguments, their bickering and banter. I especially loved that even as they sank knee-deep in the danger and tangled web of clues, they could still laugh and have fun. They just bounced off one another so well and I cannot wait to see their romance deepen further!<br /><br />The secondary characters are all just as gripping. From the smooth, suave Sylvain - who despite his charming first impressions, felt rather sly to me from the beginning - to the bubbly, energetic Jo who's hiding troubling secrets of her own. And I adored Rachel and Lucas! The best thing about them all was no matter how endearing or horrible they may seem, none are black and white. They are all flawed and layered and you have no idea who to really trust, because you're almost certain to get it wrong. Some whose early acts prove they're complete jerks, turn out to have a shred of humanity in them after all. Or else those you think you CAN trust.... well, you see my point? It's so realistic because as humans we're all trustworthy to a point, but sometimes we break that trust or do things that make us seem like jerks. No one person is ALL good or bad and I felt Christi pulled that off brilliantly with her characters.<br /><br />What I loved most about this book was how unpredictable it was. I had no idea whether there was something paranormal going on or else was it.... SOMETHING?! Not until around 3/4 of the way through did I start unraveling the mystery and even then, I wasn't entirely certain. There's this uneasy feeling you get throughout the whole novel. Much like when you can sense a predator lurking behind you on a dark street, but you can't see them. You've no idea if someone is really there or if it's just your imagination. Night School was exactly like that, your instincts are on high alert, but you can't pinpoint the cause of it.<br /><br />Christi has weaved together such a compelling novel that will have you guessing the entire way, with characters who will spin you in so many different directions, you'll be breathless and dizzy by the time you finish. In the dark and eerie quiet of the woods, who is friend and who is predator? Follow your instincts, because that's the only help you'll find. Night School is a thrilling start to a series I am so eager to discover more of!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10699822805409365942" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1357228932" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1357228932" />
    <a title="Emily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16362475-emily"><img alt="Emily" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559946867p2/16362475.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1357228932?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/16362475-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1357228932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12142696307766806717">Night School was just a random buy at a store a couple of days ago. Actually, it wasn't exactly a "buy". Bascially I got it for free, so why the heck would I not grab it with me home? I read the blurb, which sounded interesting, and I honestly could use me some fantasy/boarding school kind of shiz right now.<br/><br/>Boarding school I got, but a fantasy it was not. Neither was it a mystery or paranormal. Then what was it, you probably ask, and I truthfully am not sure. Most of the story revolves around Al</span>
  <span id="freeText12142696307766806717" style="display:none">Night School was just a random buy at a store a couple of days ago. Actually, it wasn't exactly a "buy". Bascially I got it for free, so why the heck would I not grab it with me home? I read the blurb, which sounded interesting, and I honestly could use me some fantasy/boarding school kind of shiz right now.<br /><br />Boarding school I got, but a fantasy it was not. Neither was it a mystery or paranormal. Then what was it, you probably ask, and I truthfully am not sure. Most of the story revolves around Allie adapting to the boarding school life, making friends, picking out her outfit for the ball and worrying about boys. Sure, there where some moments throughout the book with a slight mystery-element to it, and we were told from early on that there was something going on in the school.<br /><br />You don't really get any answers though, so the book just dragged and dragged and dragged... and even when we do get answers (at page 400 or so) it's so anti-climatic, unrealistic and plain that at first I couldn't believe my own eyes. I continued reading thinking that the "real" answers were in the next chapter, or that some new twist would change my view on the whole big reveal. But then eventually I got to the last page and no such twist had come, and I just sat there.<br /><br />I just sat there, not sure what I was supposed to think. I'm not gonna lie, there's not much in that book to have an opinion on. There's not much happening. <br /><br />The actual book and my first impression of it, the way it makes itself sound is so different that it almost makes me laugh. I mean, take the title and the blurb. It's called Night School, and is about a boarding school that is hiding a secret. Am I the only one who thinks that screams VAMPIRES or something similar? Then when you open the book and read, even then it deceives you. The atmosphere is strangely paranormal-ish, with strange and unexplainable things happening to our main character. <br /><br />I dont know guys, maybe the author started the book without really knowing where it was going. Maybe she just wrote and wrote what she thought was an intriguing plot, and then after a while she was like "oh crap, I don't even know how I'm gonna end it" and just decided to write some random stuff she came up with while pouring herself some cereal. <br /><br />Which made a very paranormal-ish book get a really ... normal? ending. Normal in the sense that it was nothing supernatural, I mean. <br /><br />You know what this book is like? It's like when you're home alone and it's dark outside, and you keep hearing footsteps and scratching and you're 100% sure there's someone in the house with you. Maybe a ghost, or an axe murderer, and wait, did you forget to lock the door earlier today? And you walk around, heart beating in your chest, blood thumping in your ears, trying to pinpoint where the sound is coming from. <br /><br />Then you realize it's from one of the bedrooms, so you stretch out your hand, shaking, to open the door. When it creaks open, your cat leaps out, and you realize there was really nothing to worry about.<br /><br />That's how this book was.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12142696307766806717" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer272945459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13663375635928657549">This was like an awesome mix of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/345627.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy___1_' title='Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy, #1) by Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a>,<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1629601.The_Disreputable_History_of_Frankie_Landau_Banks' title='The Disreputable History of Frankie Landau-Banks by E. Lockhart' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1313980820s/1629601.jpg' alt='The Disreputable History of Frankie Landau-Banks by E. Lockhart' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a>,<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8527908.Haven__Winterhaven___1_' title='Haven (Winterhaven, #1) by Kristi Cook' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1322418746s/8527908.jpg' alt='Haven (Winterhaven, #1) by Kristi Cook' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/872333.Blue_Bloods__Blue_Bloods___1_' title='Blue Bloods (Blue Bloods, #1) by Melissa de la Cruz' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1322281515s/872333.jpg' alt='Blue Bloods (Blue Bloods, #1) by Melissa de la Cruz' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a>. So, obviously if you liked any of these I would suggest you pick up this one. <br/><br/>While I am saying this was a mix of those it also was original in it's own ways. I was thinking I was sort of over the whole boarding school thing, but this one sucked me in. It was a really different school, so I didn't get bored with the setting. <br/><br/><br/>Allie is trouble with a capital T since her brother, Christopher went missing. She has pulled her last stunt and her</span>
  <span id="freeText13663375635928657549" style="display:none">This was like an awesome mix of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/345627.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy___1_" title="Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy, #1) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1331231240s/345627.jpg" alt="Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy, #1) by Richelle Mead" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>,<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1629601.The_Disreputable_History_of_Frankie_Landau_Banks" title="The Disreputable History of Frankie Landau-Banks by E. Lockhart" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1313980820s/1629601.jpg" alt="The Disreputable History of Frankie Landau-Banks by E. Lockhart" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>,<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8527908.Haven__Winterhaven___1_" title="Haven (Winterhaven, #1) by Kristi Cook" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1322418746s/8527908.jpg" alt="Haven (Winterhaven, #1) by Kristi Cook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/872333.Blue_Bloods__Blue_Bloods___1_" title="Blue Bloods (Blue Bloods, #1) by Melissa de la Cruz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1322281515s/872333.jpg" alt="Blue Bloods (Blue Bloods, #1) by Melissa de la Cruz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>. So, obviously if you liked any of these I would suggest you pick up this one. <br><br>While I am saying this was a mix of those it also was original in it's own ways. I was thinking I was sort of over the whole boarding school thing, but this one sucked me in. It was a really different school, so I didn't get bored with the setting. <br><br><br>Allie is trouble with a capital T since her brother, Christopher went missing. She has pulled her last stunt and her parents decide to send her to a new "school", Cimmera. It was all very rushed and secretive. No one gets into this school unless they are super gifted or a legacy. Allie is neither, that she is aware of. Even though the school is weird and she is away from her family, she starts to really like it there. She meets new friends and crushes. Everything seems to be going smooth, until her new friend Jo and her hear a growling noise and are saved by Gabe and Sylivain. Things are very secretive. There is a "night school" for certain kids, whom can't talk about it and who have to be invited to join. Fishy? When Allie and Carter overhear some disturbing news Allie is worried for her safety and discovers some things about her past.<br><br><br><br>Warning: this ends on quite the cliffhanger. I wan't book #2 right NOW!<br><br><br>Spoilers:<br><br>I was not suprised about Gabe. He was never super nice to Allie. <br>I still am wondering what power he had over Jo? Compulsion?<br><br>Given the name is Night School I was thinking we'd have some vampire moments.... But, we didn't?????? <br><br>At the Summer Ball did anyone else get a Fairy vibe? The dancing, the drinking????<br><br>I am really wondering if some supernatural moments are coming for us in #2......<br><br><br><br>Great read. I had fun. I am excited for the next book. All in all, I have to give this one 4 stars.<br><br><br>Thanks Tina for sharing! I love me some street corner bookers!!!</span>

I was roaming in my Goodreads page and saw one of my friends reading the fifth book on this series so I went and checked the first one. <div id="review_219160834" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/219160834" />
    <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life"><img alt="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563622982p2/3024878.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/219160834?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life">Donna {Book Passion For Life}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=ya-dystopian-scifi-thriller">ya-dystopian-scifi-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer219160834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5623786148322637946">As soon as I seen the <i>Night School</i> book cover on Goodreads I knew I wanted to read it, I mean just look at it, it’s gorgeous. Not only that but it has a very intriguing blub and so I knew I had to get it. Now let me tell you, after reading it Night School is a mysterious, thrilling and dangerous ride, one that will leave readers guessing to the very end and I loved it!<br/><br/>Allie Sheridan’s life was perfect, well that was until her older brother Christopher disappeared one day leaving only a note to s</span>
  <span id="freeText5623786148322637946" style="display:none">As soon as I seen the <i>Night School</i> book cover on Goodreads I knew I wanted to read it, I mean just look at it, it’s gorgeous. Not only that but it has a very intriguing blub and so I knew I had to get it. Now let me tell you, after reading it Night School is a mysterious, thrilling and dangerous ride, one that will leave readers guessing to the very end and I loved it!<br /><br />Allie Sheridan’s life was perfect, well that was until her older brother Christopher disappeared one day leaving only a note to saying not to look for him. Not knowing where her brother was had a huge affect on Allie and so she turned from good girl to bad girl and ends up getting herself in trouble with the police several times. However, after the third time Allie’s parents decide to send her to Cimmeria Academy, a legacy school where the best and richest students go to try and sort her out.<br /><br />During her time at Cimmeria Academy, Allie quickly makes friends and starts to enjoy it there but when strange things start happening she can’t help notice that things aren’t what they seem. Everyone seems to be hiding secrets that involve the Night School students; a group of selected students whose activates aren’t even talked about. But when one of her classmates is murdered at the summer ball and rumours start flying that Allie was involved, she soon becomes determined to find out what’s going on a Cimmeria Academy…..but who can she trust and what secret’s will she reveal?<br /><br /><i>Night School</i> is the first book in a new and exciting series by author CJ Daughtery and I know this will be a hit amongst the readers. From the very start you’re thrown in a mysterious and dangerous world and it is easy to love it. I admit I did feel the first 100 pages moved pretty slowly but I now realise that this was done so we got to know Allie and got the feel for Cimmeria Academy before the story really kicks off. We get to know a lot of characters, some nice and some not and they all play a key part in the story, especially the Night School students. I have to say trying to figure out what their group was involved with was a complete mystery. I even turned to thinking that maybe this was a paranormal book because I just couldn’t figure it out, but eventually everything was revealed and I thought it was an excellent twist.<br /><br />One of my favourite things in this book was the characters, they are so loveable. Allie is a fantastic character, she’s smart, she’s funny and she doesn’t let anyone walk all over her. When Katie tries to pick on her she quickly speaks up and doesn’t take any crap. Then there’s Jo, Lucas and Rachel, who are all very loyal friends to Allie and my favourite amongst the three has to be Lucas. Even though he’s involved with the <i>Night School</i> he’s still Allie’s friend even when everyone else turns against her. But then we have Carter. He was one tough guy! He’s so moody and broody to start with that you can’t help love him and it was pretty obvious that he liked Allie. He and Allie have a few touching scenes together and you truly see their romance develop. It’s actually really sweet and I loved how he was will to do whatever to help Allie. It’s safe to say I can’t wait to see what comes next with them. One character I really didn’t like was Sylvain, he was creepy and sleazy and if I was Allie, I wouldn’t have forgiven him but she did.<br /><br />Overall, CJ Daugherty has done a great job with <i>Night School</i> and if you’re looking for something new, exciting and fresh, then this is the book for you. I can’t wait for the next instalment and I’m praying it comes soon.<br /><br /><i>Thank you to Atom for giving me the opportunity to review this book.</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="5623786148322637946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_398539995" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/398539995" />
    <a title="Sandra " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9752625-sandra"><img alt="Sandra " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345749155p2/9752625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/398539995?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra " href="/user/show/9752625-sandra">Sandra </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=reviewed-books">reviewed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=nooo-way">nooo-way</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=liked-the-characters-some-or-all">liked-the-characters-some-or-all</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sexy-males">sexy-males</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer398539995" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17988372758776588890">Love, love, love it!!! it was awasome and i couldnt put it down! many hilarious, romantic and exciting scenes that made the reader gasping for more. i mean what more do you need? it definitely has everything a reader wants.<br/><br/>My favorite characters are Allie and Carter. Infact i liked ALL the characters. They were well described and developed and you get to know them more in the middle of the book.<br/><br/>What can i say about the love triangles? i will describe them in 3 different words. unique, loving and</span>
  <span id="freeText17988372758776588890" style="display:none">Love, love, love it!!! it was awasome and i couldnt put it down! many hilarious, romantic and exciting scenes that made the reader gasping for more. i mean what more do you need? it definitely has everything a reader wants.<br /><br />My favorite characters are Allie and Carter. Infact i liked ALL the characters. They were well described and developed and you get to know them more in the middle of the book.<br /><br />What can i say about the love triangles? i will describe them in 3 different words. unique, loving and romantic. i absolutely love them!!! Especially the love triangle between Carter, Allie and Sylvain ( the main characters). Its a genius idea to put Allie first with Sylvain and then with Carter couse we get to see Allie with both of them.<br /><br />I think that the beggining of the book was really amazing and exciting. you immediately get hooked in and it doesnt bore you to death like in some books but it makes you think " OMG, THIS BOOK IS THE BEST BOOK EVER!!! THANK GOD I BROUGHT IT!!!"<br /><br />This book was different from others because, well, Allie was different ( main character). It wosnt like it was with other books. That the main character's parents died and they had to live with their uncle/ aunty or that their parents are divorced or are going to.<br /><br />In the book Allie's parents are together but they're not as good and perfect as they used to be because Allie's older brother, who's name is Christopher, run away from home. Allie and Christopher were super close and they were best friends since forever. So when she finds out that Christopher run away and left her she kinda has a breakdown. She starts to get into a big amounts of trouble nearly everyday and gets these panick or anger attacks. You name it. She also gets arrested 3 times in a year. Because of that her parents get really tired of her and cant handle her anymore, so they decide to set her of to Cimmeria ( a secret boarding school).<br /><br />The ending left me breathless. Night school is now one of my favorite books and i cant wait to read the second book!!! If you're a fan of Born At Midnight or The Vampire Diaries and love mystery, romance and adventure then you should buy this book right now.I definitely recommend this magnificent book!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17988372758776588890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1769475591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13750397738212270806">Night scool was such a fun read. There were a lot of characters, but everybody had their moment to shine. There was a lot of character development as well. We saw a brat at the begging turning into a woman at the end. So much drama, so much twist and so much swear words (which is a bonus) this was everything I wanted into a fun YA book. I like how there is a end to a story but also a opening to a lot of things to come. C.J. is a great author.<br/><br/>5 zvezdica od mene, hvala Laguni sto nema cudne prevod</span>
  <span id="freeText13750397738212270806" style="display:none">Night scool was such a fun read. There were a lot of characters, but everybody had their moment to shine. There was a lot of character development as well. We saw a brat at the begging turning into a woman at the end. So much drama, so much twist and so much swear words (which is a bonus) this was everything I wanted into a fun YA book. I like how there is a end to a story but also a opening to a lot of things to come. C.J. is a great author.<br /><br />5 zvezdica od mene, hvala Laguni sto nema cudne prevode kad neki drugi izdavaci! Jedva cekam da zapocnem Nasledje!</span>

<div id="review_977062222" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/977062222" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/977062222?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna (Enchanted by YA)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna (Enchanted by YA)" href="/user/show/30983445-anna-enchanted-by-ya">Anna (Enchanted by YA)</a>
      </span>

          marked it as did-not-finish




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer977062222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17925316223609222136">Everything about this book - from the title, to the cover, to the synopsis - <i>screams</i> paranormal romance/mystery. So to find out (after I'd already started) that it was nothing of the sort... safe to say I was disappointed.<br/>When I was checking this out in other people's reviews I also noticed that a lot of things to come simply weren't my cup of tea, so adding that to a poor start meant this is a non-finisher for me.<br/>Maybe I'll pick it back up another time, but it's unlikely.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7U48NsM1D2eddemC79TStwyW/9ku+si8P45Zs/y3mWcoXmotY+PfyBKokYmfo4yBA2D4YNMNHvZspjwC7cjsHg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5M1NS44Ysr3J/XhZrbtvzFmLCUFtAedHHRO/05LJ4d0h3RtQLs5iEkYgAFLdzDH6Vn0O+JD2MQ1OO9pig7aUpA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
